# Analysis

## Ground Truth (GT)

The GT expression is:
$$f(P) = 0.5980 \cdot (1 - P/32.939) \cdot P + 0.5980 \cdot (1 - \exp(-0.0768 \cdot P)) \cdot P$$

Expanding:
$$f(P) = 0.5980 \cdot P - 0.5980 \cdot P^2/32.939 + 0.5980 \cdot P - 0.5980 \cdot P \cdot \exp(-0.0768 \cdot P)$$

$$f(P) = 1.196 \cdot P - 0.01815 \cdot P^2 - 0.5980 \cdot P \cdot \exp(-0.0768 \cdot P)$$

So the GT has the form:
$$f(P) = a \cdot P^2 + b \cdot P + c \cdot P \cdot \exp(d \cdot P)$$

where $a < 0$, $b > 0$, $c < 0$, $d < 0$.

**Key structural observation:** GT is a function of P only (no t dependence), and consists of basis functions: $P^2$, $P$, and $P \cdot \exp(d \cdot P)$.

## Checking Candidates

Let me check which candidates match the form $a \cdot P^2 + b \cdot P + c \cdot P \cdot \exp(d \cdot P)$ (with possible additive constant = 0).

**Candidate 9:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(P*c4)`

This simplifies to: $c_0 P^2 + (c_1 + c_2) P + c_3 P \exp(c_4 P)$

This is exactly the form $a P^2 + b P + c P \exp(d P)$ with:
- $c_0 = -0.01815$
- $c_1 + c_2 = 1.196$
- $c_3 = -0.5980$
- $c_4 = -0.0768$

**This is an exact match!** ✓

**Candidate 10:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P + c4`

This is $c_0 P^2 + (c_1 + 1) P + c_2 P \exp(c_3 P) + c_4$. The extra constant $c_4$ can be set to 0. This matches. ✓

**Candidate 11:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4` — Set $c_4 = 0$. Matches. ✓

**Candidate 12:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(P*c4) + c5` — Set $c_5 = 0$. Same as Candidate 9 + constant. Matches. ✓

**Candidate 13:** Same as 12 with extra $P \cdot c_5$ term, which merges into the linear P term. Matches. ✓

**Candidate 5:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P + c4*exp(P*c3) + c5` — Has an extra $c_4 \exp(c_3 P)$ term (not multiplied by P). This is a different basis function from $P \exp(dP)$. Cannot be zeroed unless $c_4 = 0$. Setting $c_4 = 0, c_5 = 0$ gives the right form. ✓

**Candidate 6:** Extra $c_5 \exp(c_4 P)$ — set $c_5 = 0, c_6 = 0$. Matches. ✓

**Candidates 17-27:** These involve $t$ dependence. Setting the $t$-dependent coefficients to 0 reduces them to the core form. For example, Candidate 17: set $c_6 = 0$, then it's Candidate 12. ✓

Many candidates match by zeroing extra terms. The cleanest exact match is **Candidate 9**.

For candidates with $P^{c}$ terms (like Candidates 1, 7, 8, etc.), setting $c_1 = 2$ (for $P^{c_1}$) would give $P^2$ which merges with existing $P^2$ terms, and the remaining structure could match. These also work.

Since Candidate 9 is an exact structural match with the GT (no need to zero any constants), and many others match by zeroing extra terms:

= 0.598*P - 0.598*P²/32.94 + 0.598*P - 0.598*P*exp(-0.0768*P)
= 0.598*P - 0.01816*P² + 0.598*P - 0.598*P*exp(-0.0768*P)
= 1.196*P - 0.01816*P² - 0.598*P*exp(-0.0768*P)
